        <script>
            var $trigger = $('.js-category-trigger'), $footer = $('.js-footer'), $back = $('.js-back'), $categories = $('.js-category');

            function setCategory(target) {
                var $picked = $categories.filter('[data-name="' + target + '"]');
                $categories.removeClass('_visible');
                $picked.addClass('_visible');
            }

            $trigger.on('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();

                var target = $(this).data('target');

                $trigger.removeClass('_active');
                $(this).addClass('_active');

                $footer.addClass('_is-category-open');
                setCategory(target);
            });

            $back.on('click', function (e) {
                e.preventDefault();

                $trigger.removeClass('_active');
                $footer.removeClass('_is-category-open');

                setCategory('default');
            });
        </script>
